| ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠ | ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ |
|------|---------|
| `app` | application name |
| `tier` | application tier (frontend, backend, etc.) |
| `env` | environment (dev, staging, prod) |
| `rel` | release version |
| `component` | ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö |
| `partition` | partition identifier |

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:
```bash
# ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å pods ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ selector
kubectl get pods -l app=nginx,env=production
```

#### 5.4.5 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Context ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤

| ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠ | ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏° | ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ |
|---------|----------|---------|
| `k config get-contexts` | `kubectl config get-contexts` | ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ contexts ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î |
| `k config current-context` | `kubectl config current-context` | ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á context ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà |
| `k config use-context` | `kubectl config use-context` | ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô context ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô |

#### 5.4.6 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô YAML Manifest

| ‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠ | ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ |
|---------|---------|
| `apiVersion` | ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á API ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£ |
| `kind` | ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£ |
| `metadata` | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô name, namespace, labels |
| `spec` | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£ |
| `replicas` | ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô replicas ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ |
| `selector` | ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å pods |
| `template` | ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á pods |
| `containers` | ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á containers ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á pod |
| `volumeMounts` | ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ mount volumes ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà container |
| `env` | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ environment variables |
| `resources` | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô (CPU, memory) |

## 6. üìà ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Scale ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Update ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô

### 6.1 ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Scale ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô
```bash
# Scale deployment ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô 5 replicas
kubectl scale deployment nginx-deployment --replicas=5

# ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå YAML ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß apply ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
```

### Horizontal Pod Autoscaler (HPA)

HPA ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢ scale ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô pods ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£
```yaml
# my-hpa.yaml
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: nginx-hpa
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: nginx-deployment
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 50
```

```bash
kubectl apply -f my-hpa.yaml
kubectl get hpa
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Update ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô
```bash
# Update image ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á deployment
kubectl set image deployment/nginx-deployment nginx=nginx:1.16.1

# ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ roll out
kubectl rollout history deployment/nginx-deployment

# Roll back ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤
kubectl rollout undo deployment/nginx-deployment
```

## 7. üåê ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥ Networking ‡πÉ‡∏ô Kubernetes

### 7.1 Service Types

1. **ClusterIP** - ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô cluster
2. **NodePort** - ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î port ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å node ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å
3. **LoadBalancer** - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ load balancer ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ cloud
4. **ExternalName** - ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á CNAME DNS record

### 7.2 Ingress

Ingress ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö HTTP/HTTPS

#### 7.2.1 Ingress ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?

Ingress ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Kubernetes resource ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Services ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô cluster ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô layer 7 (HTTP/HTTPS) load balancer ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ reverse proxy ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ:

1. **‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ HTTP routing** - ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á services ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° URL path ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ subdomain
2. **SSL/TLS termination** - ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ TLS
3. **Name-based virtual hosting** - ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÇ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô IP ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
4. **Load balancing** - ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á services ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ

#### 7.2.2 Ingress Controller ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?

Ingress ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏é‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ traffic ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£ ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ **Ingress Controller** ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏é‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Ingress Controller ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:

- **NGINX Ingress Controller** - ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ô NGINX web server
- **Traefik** - ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ microservices
- **HAProxy** - High Availability Proxy
- **Kong** - API Gateway ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ô NGINX
- **Istio Ingress** - ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Istio service mesh
- **AWS ALB Ingress** - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Application Load Balancer ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á AWS

#### 7.2.3 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Ingress

‡∏™‡∏°‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏°‡∏µ microservices ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ã‡∏ï‡πå ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ã:

- `web-frontend` - UI ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ã‡∏ï‡πå
- `api-products` - API ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤
- `api-orders` - API ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏ã‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠
- `api-users` - API ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
- `admin-dashboard` - ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö

‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å deploy ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Deployment ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ Service ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á

**‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 1: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ã‡∏ï‡πå‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ã‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ path-based routing**

1. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Ingress**:
   ```yaml
   apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
   kind: Ingress
   metadata:
     name: ecommerce-ingress
     annotations:
       nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/rewrite-target: /
   spec:
     rules:
     - host: shop.example.com
       http:
         paths:
         - path: /
           pathType: Prefix
           backend:
             service:
               name: web-frontend
               port:
                 number: 80
         - path: /api/products
           pathType: Prefix
           backend:
             service:
               name: api-products
               port:
                 number: 8080
         - path: /api/orders
           pathType: Prefix
           backend:
             service:
               name: api-orders
               port:
                 number: 8080
         - path: /api/users
           pathType: Prefix
           backend:
             service:
               name: api-users
               port:
                 number: 8080
     - host: admin.example.com
       http:
         paths:
         - path: /
           pathType: Prefix
           backend:
             service:
               name: admin-dashboard
               port:
                 number: 80
     tls:
     - hosts:
       - shop.example.com
       - admin.example.com
       secretName: example-tls-secret
   ```

2. **‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô**:
   - ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏° `https://shop.example.com`
   - DNS ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á traffic ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á public IP ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Ingress Controller
   - Ingress Controller ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Host header ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö `shop.example.com`
   - ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á root path (`/`), traffic ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á `web-frontend` service
   - ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á `/api/products`, Ingress ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏á traffic ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á `api-products` service

3. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ TLS**:
   - Ingress ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Secret ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ `example-tls-secret` ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á TLS ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ private key
   - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ HTTPS ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà Ingress Controller (TLS termination)
   - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Ingress Controller ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ backend services ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô HTTP ‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≤ (‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô cluster)

**‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 2: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Blue-Green Deployment**

1. **‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï `api-products` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà**:
   - Deploy `api-products-v2` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Service ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
   - ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö `api-products-v2` ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ internal testing
   - ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï Ingress rule ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô traffic ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `api-products` ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà `api-products-v2`:

   ```yaml
   - path: /api/products
     pathType: Prefix
     backend:
       service:
         name: api-products-v2
         port:
           number: 8080
   ```

2. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Rollback ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤**:
   - ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç Ingress ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
   - ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô backend service ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô `api-products`
   - ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ rollback

**‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 3: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Traffic ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Canary**

1. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô**:
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ annotations ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Ingress Controller ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á traffic:
   ```yaml
   metadata:
     annotations:
       nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/canary: "true"
       nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/canary-weight: "20"
   ```

   - ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á 20% ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á traffic ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
   - ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÜ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ weight ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏±‡πà‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡∏µ

#### 7.2.4 ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Ingress

##### 7.2.4.1 ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥ ‚úÖ

1. **‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å Ingress Controller ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°**
   - ‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô performance, ‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Ingress Controller ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö cloud provider ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤

2. **‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á URL ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ö**
   - ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á URL ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á microservices
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ path prefixes ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `/api/v1/` ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö API ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô 1

3. **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Annotations ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°**
   - Ingress Controllers ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ annotations ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ
   ```yaml
   annotations:
     nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-body-size: "10m"
     nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"
   ```

### 7.3 Network Policies

Network Policies ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á pods
```yaml
# network-policy.yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: NetworkPolicy
metadata:
  name: access-nginx
spec:
  podSelector:
    matchLabels:
      app: nginx
  ingress:
  - from:
  ingress:
  - from:
    - podSelector:
        matchLabels:
          access: "true"
    ports:
    - protocol: TCP
      port: 80
```

## 8. üíæ ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Persistent Volumes

### Persistent Volume (PV) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Persistent Volume Claim (PVC)

PV ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà admin ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ PVC ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
```yaml
# persistent-volume.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: PersistentVolume
metadata:
  name: my-pv
spec:
  capacity:
    storage: 1Gi
  accessModes:
    - ReadWriteOnce
  hostPath:
    path: "/mnt/data"
```
```yaml
# persistent-volume-claim.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: PersistentVolumeClaim
metadata:
  name: my-pvc
spec:
  accessModes:
    - ReadWriteOnce
  resources:
    requests:
      storage: 500Mi
```
```bash
kubectl apply -f persistent-volume.yaml
kubectl apply -f persistent-volume-claim.yaml

# ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö PV ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ PVC
kubectl get pv
kubectl get pvc
```

### 8.1 ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ PVC ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Pod

```yaml
# pod-with-pvc.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
metadata:
  name: nginx-pvc-pod
spec:
  containers:
  - name: nginx
    image: nginx
    volumeMounts:
    - mountPath: "/usr/share/nginx/html"
      name: nginx-data
  volumes:
  - name: nginx-data
    persistentVolumeClaim:
      claimName: my-pvc
```

### 8.2 ConfigMaps ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Secrets



#### 8.2.1 ConfigMap

ConfigMap ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Kubernetes resource ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• configuration ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö key-value ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö

**‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:**
- ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å configuration ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô (Configuration externalization)
- ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• configuration ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô URLs, port numbers, feature flags
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß, ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå configuration ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å directory

**‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤:**
1. **‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å Configuration ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î**: ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å 12-Factor App ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà configuration ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î
2. **‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ConfigMap ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° (dev, staging, production)
3. **‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á image ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö configuration ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á rebuild container image
4. **‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏î‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ deploy**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö configuration ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö Kubernetes ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î

**‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô ConfigMap:**

1. **‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ConfigMap**:
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: app-config
data:
  database_url: "mysql://db:3306/mydb"
  app_mode: "production"
  cache_ttl: "300"
  config.properties: |
    app.name=MyApplication
    app.description=Example Application
    log.level=INFO
```

2. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ConfigMap ‡πÉ‡∏ô Pod**:
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
metadata:
  name: config-demo-pod
spec:
  containers:
  - name: app
    image: myapp:1.0
    env:
    # ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î key ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô environment variables
    - name: DB_URL
      valueFrom:
        configMapKeyRef:
          name: app-config
          key: database_url
    # ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ConfigMap ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô environment variables
    envFrom:
    - configMapRef:
        name: app-config
    volumeMounts:
    # ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î ConfigMap ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå
    - name: config-volume
      mountPath: /etc/config
  volumes:
  - name: config-volume
    configMap:
      name: app-config
```

**Best Practices ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ConfigMap:**

1. **‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ key ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢**: ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô
2. **‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà**: ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å ConfigMap ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
3. **‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ GitOps**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö ConfigMap ‡πÉ‡∏ô version control ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á
4. **‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î**: ConfigMap ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î 1MB ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ resource
5. **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ immutable ConfigMaps**: ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ `immutable: true` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏à
6. **‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô ConfigMap**: ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ ConfigMap ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á

#### 8.2.2 Secret

Secret ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Kubernetes resource ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö

**‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:**
- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô passwords, OAuth tokens, SSH keys
- ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô base64 (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢)
- ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Secret ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö: Opaque (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô), TLS, docker-registry, bootstrap token

**‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤:**
1. **‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î**: ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô source code
2. **‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ RBAC ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á Secrets ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
3. **‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö**: ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á credentials ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á image ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
4. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö credentials ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢

**‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô Secret:**

1. **‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Secret**:
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Secret
metadata:
  name: app-secrets
type: Opaque
data:
  # ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ base64
  username: YWRtaW4=  # base64 encoded "admin"
  password: cGFzc3dvcmQxMjM=  # base64 encoded "password123"
stringData:
  # ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ base64
  config.json: |
    {
      "apiKey": "xyz123",
      "authDomain": "example.com"
    }
```

2. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Secret ‡πÉ‡∏ô Pod**:
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
metadata:
  name: secret-demo-pod
spec:
  containers:
  - name: app
    image: myapp:1.0
    env:
    # ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î key ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô environment variables
    - name: DB_USERNAME
      valueFrom:
        secretKeyRef:
          name: app-secrets
          key: username
    # ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Secret ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô environment variables
    envFrom:
    - secretRef:
        name: app-secrets
    volumeMounts:
    # ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î Secret ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå
    - name: secret-volume
      mountPath: /etc/secrets
      readOnly: true
  volumes:
  - name: secret-volume
    secret:
      secretName: app-secrets
```

**Best Practices ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Secret:**

1. **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö Secrets ‡πÉ‡∏ô Version Control**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö template ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ tools ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Sealed Secrets, SOPS
2. **‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ Secrets ‡πÉ‡∏ô etcd**: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ Secrets ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô etcd
3. **‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ RBAC**: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á Secrets ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏î
4. **‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô Secrets ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≥**: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô credentials
5. **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ External Secrets Managers**: ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ secrets ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô HashiCorp Vault, AWS Secrets Manager
6. **‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Pod Security Context**: ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á volume ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ secrets ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å containers ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
7. **‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ imagePullSecrets** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á images ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å private repositories
8. **‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Secret Type ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `kubernetes.io/tls` ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö certificates

**‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ConfigMap ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Secret:**

| ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏∞ | ConfigMap | Secret |
|----------|-----------|--------|
| ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏õ | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö |
| ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™ | ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ base64 |
| ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• | ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏£‡∏µ‡πà‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ etcd | ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏£‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢ |
| ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î | 1MB | 1MB |
| ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô | environment variables, files | environment variables, files, mount ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö TLS |

## 9. üõ°Ô∏è ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Kubernetes

### RBAC (Role-Based Access Control)

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ô Kubernetes
```yaml
# role.yaml
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: Role
metadata:
  namespace: default
  name: pod-reader
rules:
- apiGroups: [""]
  resources: ["pods"]
  verbs: ["get", "watch", "list"]
```
```yaml
# role-binding.yaml
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
kind: RoleBinding
metadata:
  name: read-pods
  namespace: default
subjects:
- kind: User
  name: jane
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io
roleRef:
  kind: Role
  name: pod-reader
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io
```

#### 9.1 ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ RBAC

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph Users
        U1[Admin]
        U2[Developer]
        U3[Operator]
    end

    subgraph Roles
        R1[Cluster Admin]
        R2[Namespace Admin]
        R3[Pod Reader]
        R4[Deployment Manager]
    end

    subgraph Resources
        POD[Pods]
        DEP[Deployments]
        SVC[Services]
        SEC[Secrets]
        CM[ConfigMaps]
    end

    U1 --> R1
    U2 --> R2
    U2 --> R4
    U3 --> R3

    R1 --> POD
    R1 --> DEP
    R1 --> SVC
    R1 --> SEC
    R1 --> CM
    
    R2 --> POD
    R2 --> DEP
    R2 --> SVC
    R2 --> SEC
    R2 --> CM

    R3 --> POD
    R4 --> DEP
```

### 9.2 Pod Security Policies

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Pod
```yaml
# pod-security-policy.yaml
apiVersion: policy/v1beta1
kind: PodSecurityPolicy
metadata:
  name: restricted
spec:
  privileged: false
  seLinux:
    rule: RunAsAny
  runAsUser:
    rule: MustRunAsNonRoot
  fsGroup:
    rule: MustRunAs
    ranges:
    - min: 1000
      max: 2000
  supplementalGroups:
    rule: MustRunAs
    ranges:
    - min: 1000
      max: 2000
  volumes:
  - 'configMap'
  - 'emptyDir'
  - 'persistentVolumeClaim'
```

## 10. ‚òÅÔ∏è ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Deploy Kubernetes ‡∏ö‡∏ô Digital Ocean

Digital Ocean Kubernetes (DOKS) ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Kubernetes cluster ‡∏ö‡∏ô cloud ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏¢

### ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Setup DOKS

1. **‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ Digital Ocean** (‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ)

2. **‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á doctl CLI**
   ```bash
   # Linux
   cd ~
   wget https://github.com/digitalocean/doctl/releases/download/v1.X.X/doctl-1.X.X-linux-amd64.tar.gz
   tar xf doctl-1.X.X-linux-amd64.tar.gz
   sudo mv doctl /usr/local/bin

   # MacOS
   brew install doctl
   
   # Windows
   # ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πå‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î MSI installer ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å GitHub releases
   ```

3. **‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Digital Ocean**
   ```bash
   doctl auth init
   # ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô API token ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Digital Ocean
   ```

4. **‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Kubernetes cluster**
   ```bash
   doctl kubernetes cluster create my-cluster \
     --region sgp1 \
     --size s-2vcpu-4gb \
     --count 3
   ```

5. **‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö cluster**
   ```bash
   doctl kubernetes cluster kubeconfig save my-cluster
   kubectl get nodes
   ```

### 10.1 ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Deploy ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô DOKS

1. **‡∏ô‡∏≥ YAML manifest ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ**
   ```bash
   kubectl apply -f my-deployment.yaml
   kubectl apply -f my-service.yaml
   ```

2. **‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Load Balancer**
   ```yaml
   # lb-service.yaml
   apiVersion: v1
   kind: Service
   metadata:
     name: nginx-lb
   spec:
     selector:
       app: nginx
     ports:
     - port: 80
       targetPort: 80
     type: LoadBalancer
   ```
   ```bash
   kubectl apply -f lb-service.yaml
   kubectl get services
   # ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ IP address ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Digital Ocean
   ```

## 11. üéì ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏®‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Kubernetes ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏®‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

1. **Helm** - Package Manager ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Kubernetes
   ```bash
   # ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Helm
   curl https://raw.githubusercontent.com/helm/helm/main/scripts/get-helm-3 | bash

   # ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° repo
   helm repo add stable https://charts.helm.sh/stable
   
   # ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á chart
   helm install my-nginx stable/nginx-ingress
   ```

2. **CI/CD ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Kubernetes** - ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ArgoCD, Jenkins, GitHub Actions

3. **Service Mesh** - ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Istio
   ```bash
   # ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Istio
   istioctl install --set profile=demo
   ```

4. **‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Monitor ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Observability** - ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Prometheus, Grafana
   ```bash
   # ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Prometheus ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Helm
   helm repo add prometheus-community https://prometheus-community.github.io/helm-charts
   helm install prometheus prometheus-community/kube-prometheus-stack
   ```

5. **CKA (Certified Kubernetes Administrator)** - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Kubernetes admin
6. **CKAD (Certified Kubernetes Application Developer)** - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏ô Kubernetes
7. **CKS (Certified Kubernetes Security Specialist)** - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Kubernetes

### ‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥

- [CNCF Learning Path](https://www.cncf.io/certification/training/) - ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å CNCF
- [Kubernetes Patterns](https://k8spatterns.io/) - ‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Kubernetes
- [Kubernetes The Hard Way](https://github.com/kelseyhightower/kubernetes-the-hard-way) - ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
- [Kubernetes Documentation](https://kubernetes.io/docs/home/)
